//the following program is for finding the greater number
int a,b,c;
printf("Enter the first number\n");
scanf("%d", &a);
printf("Enter the second number\n");
scanf("%d", &b);
printf("Enter the Third number\n");
scanf("%d", &c);

if(a>b && a>c){
    printf("The first number is greater %d", a);
}
else if(b>a && b>c){
    printf("The second number is greater %d", b);
}
else{
    printf("The Third number is greater %d", c);
}
	return 0;
}

17/12/22, 10:00â€¯pm - Jay Vishwakarma Sati: Total days between 15 Dec-31 March=107 days

Total holidays for Saturday,Sunday,Monday=42 days
(Except Holi Week) 
So 107-42=65 days

Holi Vacation 6 days
65-6=59 days

Other Vacation =3
(Republic day,Sant Ravidas Jayanti, Gudipadwa) 
59-3=56 days

We will have to go college for 75%attendence
56*75/100= 42 days

So we can bunk classes for 
56-42= 14days

Total classes in December =10 days

Please note that *tonight 11:59pm* is the *deadline* for applications at *SATI Vidisha* for the Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program, an *Online Live Project* that helps students gain *Work Experience* in *Data-driven decision-making*.

The project uses a case study-driven approach, where you will assess business projects and solve problems using models used by leading firms like *Accenture, Capgemini & Cognizant*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on *real business data* to gain insights.

The project is running in leading campuses like *IIT Delhi, IIT Kanpur, IIT Bombay*, and *BITS Pilani*.

At the end of this program you will get: 
- *Certificate of Work Experience*
- *Letter of Recommendation* on performance

To apply, you can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba/application/index.php?utm_src=sativwd
*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of this project. 

*Project Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on your choice)

*Project Start*: Flexible on your schedule. 

You can also take a *break* for exams, assignments, or personal commitments as well as take an *extension* if you cannot complete it within the duration. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee: Rs. 1499 + GST

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement,
Team Finlatics

21/11/23, 11:24â€¯am - Lakshya Pawar Sati: #include <stdio.h>

// Number of processes
#define P 5

// Number of resources
#define R 3

// Function to find the need of each process
void calculateNeed(int need[P][R], int max[P][R], int alloc[P][R]) {
    for (int i = 0; i < P; i++)
        for (int j = 0; j < R; j++)
            need[i][j] = max[i][j] - alloc[i][j];
}

// Function to check if resources are available
int isSafe(int processes[P], int available[R], int max[P][R], int alloc[P][R]) {
    int need[P][R];
    calculateNeed(need, max, alloc);

    int finish[P] = {0};
    int work[R];
    for (int i = 0; i < R; i++)
        work[i] = available[i];

    int count = 0;
    while (count < P) {
        int found = 0;
        for (int p = 0; p < P; p++) {
            if (finish[p] == 0) {
                int j;
                for (j = 0; j < R; j++) {
                    if (need[p][j] > work[j])
                        break;
                }
                if (j == R) {
                    for (int k = 0; k < R; k++)
                        work[k] += alloc[p][k];

                    finish[p] = 1;
                    processes[count++] = p;
                    found = 1;
                }
            }
        }
        if (found == 0)
            return 0; // System is in an unsafe state
    }
    return 1; // System is in a safe state
}

// Function to execute Banker's algorithm
void bankerAlgorithm(int processes[P], int available[R], int max[P][R], int alloc[P][R]) {
    if (isSafe(processes, available, max, alloc)) {
        printf("Safe sequence: ");
        for (int i = 0; i < P; i++)
            printf("%d ", processes[i]);
        printf("\n");
    } else {
        printf("System is in an unsafe state.\n");
    }
}

// Example usage
int main() {
    int processes[P] = {0, 1, 2, 3, 4};
    int available[R] = {3, 3, 2};
    int max[P][R] = {{7, 5, 3}, {3, 2, 2}, {9, 0, 2}, {2, 2, 2}, {4, 3, 3}};
    int alloc[P][R] = {{0, 1, 0}, {2, 0, 0}, {3, 0, 2}, {2, 1, 1}, {0, 0, 2}};

    bankerAlgorithm(processes, available, max, alloc);

    return 0;
}
21/11/23, 11:35â€¯am - Lakshya Pawar Sati: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

// Function to find the index of the shortest seek time
int findMinSeekTime(int *queue, int head, int size, int *visited) {
    int minDistance = INT_MAX;
    int index = -1;

    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        if (!visited[i]) {
            int distance = abs(queue[i] - head);
            if (distance < minDistance) {
                minDistance = distance;
                index = i;
            }
        }
    }

    return index;
}

// Function to calculate total seek time using SSTF algorithm
int calculateTotalSeekTime(int *requestQueue, int size, int initialHead) {
    int totalSeekTime = 0;
    int currentHead = initialHead;
    int visited[size];

    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        visited[i] = 0;
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        int nextIndex = findMinSeekTime(requestQueue, currentHead, size, visited);
        visited[nextIndex] = 1;
        totalSeekTime += abs(requestQueue[nextIndex] - currentHead);
        currentHead = requestQueue[nextIndex];
    }

    return totalSeekTime;
}

// Example usage
int main() {
    int requestQueue[] = {98, 183, 37, 122, 14, 124, 65, 67};
    int size = sizeof(requestQueue) / sizeof(requestQueue[0]);
    int initialHead = 53;

    int totalSeekTime = calculateTotalSeekTime(requestQueue, size, initialHead);

    printf("Total Seek Time using SSTF: %d\n", totalSeekTime);

    return 0;
}
